### Round 3: Bahrain Grand Prix
*Date: 2005-04-03*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 13: Hungarian Grand Prix
*Date: 2005-07-31*

#### Qualifying Results
